I'm not one to give out bad reviews on a whim, but the other reviews complaining about poor customer service are unfortunately true.

I was asked many times if I needed help, but in a bad way where you're given "we think you're going to steal" vibes. I was followed and watched, and the customer service was a poorly hidden attempt to discourage me from touching anything.

The Ulta in the very same mall is much more friendly, I recommend them instead.</text>

<resp>None< /resp><review>Yes Hello. I am a master plumber and have been to Reds many times. In reviewing the comments made before this one, I can see why the customers had problems. Reds usually deals with the more professional plumbers who know the correct terms for the supplies they need. While the people who wrote their comments were sincere in their beliefs, the terms they used to request the plumbling supplies they needed were not the correct or right names they were trying to get. The term "coupler" for instance is very vague. There are several types of "couplings" in the plumbing industry, but none are called couplers.Then there is the issue of the materials they are made from. For instance, were you seeking copper, galvanized iron, black gas pipe, plastic PVC pipe, ext? As for the person who wanted the "1/2 inch nipple adapters or 1/2 inch nipple connecters", same again, adapt to what, Iron pipe, copper, adapt to a larger or smaller size? If you are not a professional, then the best way to get what you need from a supply store is to take a photo of it, or take the part to the store and show them what you need. We all live and learn. I hope this has helped you understand a complicated industry.</review></record>

< text>
I am someone who recently had horrible multi-year upper & lower implant problems. The individual I retained was well-regarded, and taught other dentists , and believe me, I shopped all around, even the big corporate place. (we all know the one)For many reasons, too many to list  here, it never seemed to go well for me.  Broken healing dentures, cracked teeth, failed implants, the list goes on and on. I was constantly in need of repairs and replacement parts. My dr. assured me I was just 1 of only 2 patients that he has had this kind of problem with. This went on for 3 and a half years !! Finally he tells me he is giving up and retiring. His insurance is going to get the bill. Well I had to scramble, because the lower implants were snapping like toothpicks, that is when I found Dr.Aman Bhullar. He read my medical records and knew of the urgency of my situation. Pretty much immediately, Dr.Bhular began helping me. Lower bridge has just been repaired, much to my relief, the situation was precarious. Dr.Bhular has all the most modern up-to-date equipment, it was like a whole new world from my retired dentist. He was genuinely concerned about everything. I was having depression and anxiety about all  this . He totally alleviated it. <text>Awesome place to get a dog!! Amazing flavor and service!!< /text></record>
</dataset><record>
< Text>
An uncomplicated little place serving up hot dogs of various types: beef, buffalo, and, the one that caught my attention, veggie. Daddy's is pretty much a window under an awning with a little table in front, and I easily could have overlooked it while pumping gas at the 7-11 across the street. But the "vegetarian" part printed on the awning stood out.

So, I went there one night and got The Vanessa, a meatless dog with grilled onions, BBQ sauce, and mustard (you can order any as a veggie version, however). As promised on their website, the order was made fresh right on the spot. This particular offering wasn't huge--think store-bought size for dog and bun here--but it was delicious and hit the spot. Daddy's is a great place to grab a bite when you're bar hopping or just out and about and don't feel like eating at one of the millions of ramen places in Hillcrest. Plus, it's open until about 2 am some nights, depending on circumstances--as explained by the notice posted on the window which you can read as you wait for your food.

It's a unique part of the landscape and I hope it remains one for many years to come.< /Text>

<Rating>5<//Rating><review>My friend and I strolled up to this little hole in the wall establishment and ordered the chicago dog and the "O" dog. Both are solid choices and very different. The chicago dog had a cool, crispness to it, and the "O" dog fulfilled that super savory and rich desire. bacon lovers rejoice.

Super thoughtful side note: sometimes I forget how loud and open I talk. I was chatting with my friend about my skepticism of cream cheese being good on a hot dog -- in regards to the seattle dog. I noticed the man behind the counter motioning to me. When I came up to the counter he handed me a hot dog and instructed me to try it. guess what it was? the seattle dog! so nice of him. He also gave me the history of it originating there. in the end, I will say I dont love cream cheese in it (i feel the same way about sushi rolls) but the kind gesture was definitely appreciated.

If you are looking for a quick and easy meal on university, to fulfill a bit of guilty pleasure cravings in the closest thing san diego has for "street food," daddy's is definitely where you should be heading.<//review>< Pictures>

< text>
Disappointing is an understatement. It was a Saturday and I was in urgent need of a trim. Unfortunately my regular barber was unavailable this weekend and I had to settle for an alternate. One stylist with a walk in basis is how this barbershop was functioning on Saturday evening which was just not efficient, but I decided to wait and take the plunge.

I requested for a fade on my sides with a one and two clipper while the top to have the hair length from a three clipper with more hair in the front for styling. Nothing was achieved . The haircut was bland and for 30$ there was absolutely no styling, no fading , or any sharpness in the cut. Might as well gone to supercut or similar.

The other thing which irked me was the way the clippers, scissors, brushes, etc. were not sanitized between clients. They are all kept in a bunch on the table behind the barber who takes and uses as needed. I had a beard trim along with the haircut and hair from the clipper went into my eyes, only god knows whose hair that was. Also, my beard trim resulted in removal of most of my beard, which was clearly adding salt to an already badly injured wound.

Wish they have more barbers/stylists or provide appointments which would be more efficient. Also, wish sanitary standards are not compromised!

2 stars only for the hot towel at the end.

Not going to head here again but thankfully it's just hair and it will grow back!</text>

These guys are very clear about what their services are, what they need to do and what they will be doing once you decide what you're going to need for your car. <Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
I just went to Oil Changers on the top of the hill where Westborough turns into Sharp Park Road. Overall, I was very satisfied.

They let me bring in my own oil and filter. (Some places want to make you use their products which are sometimes not as good and over priced) I handed them the oil and the filter and they got to work right away while I waited right there in my car. Meanwhile, they also checked the tire pressure, lights and fluids and topped off whatever was low at the same time. They even brought the dipstick so I could see what the oil level was at before I left. I was in and out in only 15-20 minutes.

The fact that they were very friendly, kept me informed as they worked and did all this for $44 bucks, I would have to give them five stars for value, attention to detail and great customer service.

I will certainly be referring them to my friends.< /review>
